constituency)">York Outer</a> since 2010</div></div></div></div></div>
<p>From 1997 to 2010, the central part of the district was covered by the <a href="/wiki/City_of_York_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="City of York (UK Parliament constituency)">City of York</a> constituency, while the remainder was split between the constituencies of <a href="/wiki/Ryedale_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="Ryedale (UK Parliament constituency)">Ryedale</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selby_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="Selby (UK Parliament constituency)">Selby</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Vale_of_York_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="Vale of York (UK Parliament constituency)">Vale of York</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> These constituencies were represented by <a href="/wiki/Hugh_Bayley" title="Hugh Bayley">Hugh Bayley</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Greenway_(MP)" class="mw-redirect" title="John Greenway (MP)">John Greenway</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Grogan_(UK_politician)" class="mw-redirect" title="John Grogan (UK politician)">John Grogan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Anne_McIntosh" title="Anne McIntosh">Anne McIntosh</a> respectively.
</p><p>Following their review in 2003 of parliamentary representation in <a href="/wiki/North_Yorkshire" title="North Yorkshire">North Yorkshire</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Boundary_Commission_for_England" class="mw-redirect" title="Boundary Commission for England">Boundary Commission for England</a> recommended the creation of two new seats for the City of York, in time for the <a href="/wiki/2010_United_Kingdom_general_election" title="2010 United Kingdom general election">general election in 2010</a>. These are <a href="/wiki/York_Central_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="York Central (UK Parliament constituency)">York Central</a>, which covers the inner urban area, and is entirely surrounded by the <a href="/wiki/York_Outer_(UK_Parliament_constituency)" title="York Outer (UK Parliament constituency)">York Outer</a> constituency.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The whole of the city and local council area lies within the <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_and_the_Humber_(European_Parliament_constituency)" title="Yorkshire and the Humber (European Parliament constituency)">Yorkshire and the Humber</a> constituency of the <a href="/wiki/European_Parliament" title="European Parliament">European Parliament</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ceremonial_governance">Ceremonial governance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Ceremonial governance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>York is within the ceremonial territorial jurisdiction of the Dukedom of York which is presently held by <a href="/wiki/Prince_Andrew" class="mw-redirect" title="Prince Andrew">Prince Andrew</a>, the incumbent <a href="/wiki/Duke_of_York" title="Duke of York">Duke of York</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Geography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Areas_of_the_City_of_York" title="Areas of the City of York">Areas of the City of York</a></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Location">Location</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Location">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The city is 22 miles (35&#160;km) north-east of <a href="/wiki/Leeds" title="Leeds">Leeds</a>, and is part of the <a href="/wiki/Leeds_City_Region" title="Leeds City Region">Leeds Region</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>York lies in the <a href="/wiki/Vale_of_York" title="Vale of York">Vale of York</a>, a flat area of fertile arable land bordered by the <a href="/wiki/Pennines" title="Pennines">Pennines</a>, the <a href="/wiki/North_York_Moors" title="North York Moors">North York Moors</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Wolds" title="Yorkshire Wolds">Yorkshire Wolds</a>. The city was built at the confluence of the Rivers Ouse and Foss on a terminal <a href="/wiki/Moraine" title="Moraine">moraine</a> left by the last <a href="/wiki/Ice_Age" class="mw-redirect" title="Ice Age">Ice Age</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Hall-25_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hall-25-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:River_Ouse_and_Lendal_Bridge_from_Riverside_Walkway_-_geograph.org.uk_-_238516.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/River_Ouse_and_Lendal_Bridge_from_Riverside_Walkway_-_geograph.org.uk_-_238516.jpg/220px-River_Ouse_and_Lendal_Bridge_from_Riverside_Walkway_-_geograph.org.uk_-_238516.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/River_Ouse_and_Lendal_Bridge_from_Riverside_Walkway_-_geograph.org.uk_-_238516.jpg/330px-River_Ouse_and_Lendal_Bridge_from_Riverside_Walkway_-_geograph.org.uk_-_238516.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/34/River_Ouse_and_Lendal_Bridge_from_Riverside_Walkway_-_geograph.org.uk_-_238516.jpg 2x" data-file-width="377" data-file-height="251" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:River_Ouse_and_Lendal_Bridge_from_Riverside_Walkway_-_geograph.org.uk_-_238516.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The city's <a href="/wiki/Lendal_Bridge" class="mw-redirect" title="Lendal Bridge">Lendal Bridge</a> crosses the <a href="/wiki/River_Ouse,_Yorkshire" title="River Ouse, Yorkshire">Ouse</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg/220px-River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg/330px-River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg/440px-River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:River_Foss_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1553874.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>River Foss</div></div></div>
<p>During Roman times, the land surrounding the rivers Ouse and Foss was marshy, making the site easy to defend. The city is prone to flooding from the River Ouse, and has an extensive (and until 2015 mostly effective) network of flood defences with walls along the river, and a liftable barrier across the River Foss where it joins the Ouse at the 'Blue Bridge'. In October and November 2000, York experienced the worst flooding in 375 years; more than 300 homes were flooded.<sup id="cite_ref-dmcbflood_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dmcbflood-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> In December 2015 the flooding was more extensive and caused major disruption.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> The extreme impact led to a personal visit by Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Much land in and around the city is on flood plains too flood-prone for development other than agriculture. The <i>ings</i> are flood meadows along the Ouse, while the <i><a href="/wiki/Strays_of_York" title="Strays of York">strays</a></i> are open common grassland in various locations around the city.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Architecture">Architecture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Architecture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/York_sites_of_interest" class="mw-redirect" title="York sites of interest">York sites of interest</a> and <a href="/wiki/Medieval_parish_churches_of_York" title="Medieval parish churches of York">Medieval parish churches of York</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/York_Minster" title="York Minster">York Minster</a>, a large <a href="/wiki/Gothic_architecture" title="Gothic architecture">Gothic</a> cathedral, dominates the city.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Clifford%27s_Tower,_from_south.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Clifford%27s_Tower%2C_from_south.JPG/220px-Clifford%27s_Tower%2C_from_south.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Clifford%27s_Tower%2C_from_south.JPG/330px-Clifford%27s_Tower%2C_from_south.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Clifford%27s_Tower%2C_from_south.JPG/440px-Clifford%27s_Tower%2C_from_south.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1536" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Clifford%27s_Tower,_from_south.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Clifford%27s_Tower" class="mw-redirect" title="Clifford&#39;s Tower">Clifford's Tower</a>, part of York Castle</div></div></div> <p><a href="/wiki/York_Castle" title="York Castle">York Castle</a>, a complex of buildings ranging from the medieval Clifford's Tower to the 20th-century entrance to the <a href="/wiki/York_Castle_Museum" title="York Castle Museum">York Castle Museum</a> (formerly a prison) has had a chequered history.
</p><p>York's centre is enclosed by <a href="/wiki/York_city_walls" title="York city walls">the city's medieval walls</a>, which are a popular walk.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> These defences are the most complete in England. They have the only walls set on high ramparts and they retain all their principal gateways.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>  They incorporate part of the walls of the Roman fortress and some Norman and medieval work, as well as 19th- and 20th-century renovations.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Yorkshire&#39;s only 5-star hotel – The Grand Hotel and Spa" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg/220px-York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg/330px-York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg/440px-York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3981" data-file-height="2657" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:York_MMB_41_Cedar_Court_Grand_Hotel_and_Spa.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Grand Hotel and Spa</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Buildings_in_York_(8548).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Buildings_in_York_%288548%29.jpg/220px-Buildings_in_York_%288548%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Buildings_in_York_%288548%29.jpg/330px-Buildings_in_York_%288548%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Buildings_in_York_%288548%29.jpg/440px-Buildings_in_York_%288548%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4288" data-file-height="2848" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Buildings_in_York_(8548).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>George Hudson Street</div></div></div>
<p>The entire circuit is approximately 2.5 miles (4&#160;km), and encloses an area of 263 acres (106&#160;ha).<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> The north-east section includes a part where walls never existed, because the Norman <a href="/wiki/Moat" title="Moat">moat</a> of York Castle, formed by damming the <a href="/wiki/River_Foss" title="River Foss">River Foss</a>, also created a lake which acted as a city defence. This lake was later called the King's Fishpond, as the rights to fish belonged to the Crown.
</p><p>A feature of central York is the <a href="/wiki/Snickelways_of_York" title="Snickelways of York">Snickelways</a>, narrow pedestrian routes, many of which led towards the former market-places in Pavement and <a href="/wiki/Samson_of_Dol" title="Samson of Dol">St Sampson</a>'s Square.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/The_Shambles" title="The Shambles">The Shambles</a> is a narrow <a href="/wiki/Medieval" class="mw-redirect" title="Medieval">medieval</a> street, lined with shops, boutiques and <a href="/wiki/Tea_room" class="mw-redirect" title="Tea room">tea rooms</a>. Most of these premises were once butchers' shops, and the hooks from which carcasses were hung and the shelves on which meat was laid out can still be seen outside some of them. The street also contains the Shrine of <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Clitherow" title="Margaret Clitherow">Margaret Clitherow</a>, although it is not located in the house where she lived.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> Goodramgate has many medieval houses including the early-14th‑century <a href="/wiki/Lady_Row" title="Lady Row">Lady Row</a> built to finance a <a href="/wiki/Chantry" title="Chantry">Chantry</a>, at the edge of the churchyard of <a href="/wiki/Holy_Trinity_Church,_Goodramgate,_York" title="Holy Trinity Church, Goodramgate, York">Holy Trinity church</a>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg/220px-Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg/330px-Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg/440px-Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5184" data-file-height="3888" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Odeon_Cinema_3.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Art_Deco" title="Art Deco">Art Deco</a> style Odeon Cinema on Blossom Street</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Stonebow_House,_York.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Stonebow_House%2C_York.jpg/220px-Stonebow_House%2C_York.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Stonebow_House%2C_York.jpg/330px-Stonebow_House%2C_York.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Stonebow_House%2C_York.jpg/440px-Stonebow_House%2C_York.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5472" data-file-height="3648" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Stonebow_House,_York.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The 60s <a href="/wiki/Brutalist" class="mw-redirect" title="Brutalist">Brutalist</a>-style Stonebow House is an example of modern architecture</div></div></div>
<p>As well as the Castle Museum, the city contains numerous other museums and historic buildings such as the <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Museum" title="Yorkshire Museum">Yorkshire Museum</a> and its <a href="/wiki/Museum_Gardens" class="mw-redirect" title="Museum Gardens">Museum Gardens</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jorvik_Viking_Centre" title="Jorvik Viking Centre">Jorvik Viking Centre</a>, <a href="/wiki/York_Art_Gallery" title="York Art Gallery">York Art Gallery</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Richard_III_Experience_at_Monk_Bar" title="Richard III Experience at Monk Bar">Richard III Experience</a>, <a href="/wiki/Merchant_Adventurers%27_Hall" title="Merchant Adventurers&#39; Hall">Merchant Adventurers' Hall</a>, the reconstructed medieval house <a href="/wiki/Barley_Hall" title="Barley Hall">Barley Hall</a> (owned by the <a href="/wiki/York_Archaeological_Trust" title="York Archaeological Trust">York Archaeological Trust</a>), the 18th-century <a href="/wiki/Fairfax_House" title="Fairfax House">Fairfax House</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Mansion_House,_York" title="Mansion House, York">Mansion House</a> (the historic home of the Lord Mayor) and the so-called <a href="/wiki/Treasurer%27s_House,_York" title="Treasurer&#39;s House, York">Treasurer's House</a> (owned by the <a href="/wiki/National_Trust_for_Places_of_Historic_Interest_or_Natural_Beauty" title="National Trust for Places of Historic Interest or Natural Beauty">National Trust</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/National_Railway_Museum" title="National Railway Museum">National Railway Museum</a> is situated just beyond the station, and is home to a vast range of transport material and the largest collection of railway locomotives in the world. Included in this collection are the world's fastest steam locomotive <a href="/wiki/LNER_Class_A4_4468_Mallard" title="LNER Class A4 4468 Mallard">LNER Class A4 4468 <i>Mallard</i></a> and the world-famous <a href="/wiki/LNER_Class_A3_4472_Flying_Scotsman" title="LNER Class A3 4472 Flying Scotsman">LNER Class A3 4472 <i>Flying Scotsman</i></a>, which has been overhauled in the Museum.<sup id="cite_ref-nrmfs_91-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nrmfs-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
Although noted for its Medieval history, visitors can also gain an understanding of the Cold War through visiting the <a href="/wiki/York_Cold_War_Bunker" title="York Cold War Bunker">York Cold War Bunker</a>, former headquarters of No 20 Group of the Royal Observer Corps.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg/220px-YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg/330px-YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg/440px-YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3648" data-file-height="5472" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:YorkStWilliamsCollege1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/St_William%27s_College" title="St William&#39;s College">St William's College</a> facade. The curved wood protrusions are probably repurposed ship frames.</div></div></div>
<p>York is noted for its numerous churches and pubs. Most of the remaining churches in York are from the medieval period. <a href="/wiki/St_William%27s_College" title="St William&#39;s College">St William's College</a> behind the Minster, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Bedern_Hall&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Bedern Hall (page does not exist)">Bedern Hall</a>, off Goodramgate, are former dwelling places of the <a href="/wiki/Canon_(priest)" title="Canon (priest)">canons</a> of the York Minster.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">Climate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Climate">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>York has a <a href="/wiki/Temperate" class="mw-redirect" title="Temperate">temperate</a> climate with four distinct seasons. As with the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Vale_of_York" title="Vale of York">Vale of York</a> the city's climate is drier and warmer than the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_and_Humberside" class="mw-redirect" title="Yorkshire and Humberside">Yorkshire and Humberside</a> region. Owing to its lowland location, York is prone to frosts, fog, and cold winds during winter, spring and very early summer.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>  Snow can fall in winter from December onwards to as late as April but quickly melts. As with much of the British Isles, the weather is changeable. York experiences most sunshine from May to July, an average of six hours per day.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> With its inland location, summers are often warmer than the Yorkshire coast with temperatures of 27&#160;°C or more. Extremes recorded at the University of York campus between 1998 and 2010 include a highest temperature of 34.5&#160;°C (94.1&#160;°F) and a lowest temperature of −16.3&#160;°C (2.7&#160;°F) (Monday 6 December 2010). The most rainfall in one day was 88.4 millimetres (3.5&#160;in).<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Green_belt">Green belt</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Green belt">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
 <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/York_Green_Belt" title="York Green Belt">York Green Belt</a></div>
<p>York is bounded by a green belt area, which more rigorously manages development around the rural area of the district and portions of surrounding districts,<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> primarily to preserve the setting and historic character of York.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> The belt covers nearly all of the city district including all its outer villages, and extends into the surrounding North Yorkshire districts of <a href="/wiki/Hambleton_District" title="Hambleton District">Hambleton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harrogate_district" class="mw-redirect" title="Harrogate district">Harrogate</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ryedale" title="Ryedale">Ryedale</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Selby_District" title="Selby District">Selby</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Demography">Demography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Demography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable floatright" style="margin-left: 1em; width: 30em; font-size: 90%;" cellspacing="5">

<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="4">Ethnicity: York Local Authority compared
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Census_2011" class="mw-redirect" title="United Kingdom Census 2011">2011 UK census</a></th>
<th>York<sup id="cite_ref-UAStats_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UAStats-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></th>
<th><a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_and_the_Humber" title="Yorkshire and the Humber">Yorkshire and<br />the Humber</a><sup id="cite_ref-auto_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup></th>
<th>England<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>
</th></tr>

<p>The York <a href="/wiki/Urban_area" title="Urban area">urban area</a> (built-up area) had a population of 153,717 at the time of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Census_2011" class="mw-redirect" title="United Kingdom Census 2011">2011 UK census</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-BUA_103-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BUA-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> compared with 137,505 in 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-KS01_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KS01-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> 
The population of the <a href="/wiki/City_of_York" class="mw-redirect" title="City of York">City of York</a> (Local Authority) was 198,051 and its ethnic composition was 94.3% White, 1.2% Mixed, 3.4% Asian and 0.6% Black. York's elderly population (those 65 and over) was 16.9%, however only 13.2% were listed as retired.<sup id="cite_ref-UAStats_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UAStats-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="box-Update plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="Ambox current red.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" decoding="async" width="42" height="34" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="290" /></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section needs to be <b>updated</b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">November 2018</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Also at the time of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Census_2001" class="mw-redirect" title="United Kingdom Census 2001">2001 UK census</a>, the City of York had a total population of 181,094 of whom 93,957 were female and 87,137 were male. Of the 76,920 households in York, 36.0% were married couples living together, 31.3% were one-person households, 8.7% were <a href="/wiki/Cohabitation" title="Cohabitation">co-habiting</a> couples and 8.0% were lone parents. The figures for lone parent households were below the national average of 9.5%, and the percentage of married couples was also close to the national average of 36.5%; the proportion of one person households was slightly higher than the national average of 30.1%.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2001, the population density was 4,368/km<sup>2</sup> (11,310/sq&#160;mi).<sup id="cite_ref-KS01_104-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KS01-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> Of those aged 16–74 in York, 24.6% had no academic qualifications, a little lower than 28.9% in all of England. Of York's residents, 5.1% were born outside the United Kingdom, significantly lower than the national average of 9.2%. <a href="/wiki/White_British" title="White British">White British</a> form 95% of the population; the largest single minority group was recorded as Asian, at 1.9% of the population.
</p><p>The number of theft-from-a-vehicle offences and theft of a vehicle per 1,000 of the population was 8.8 and 2.7, compared to the English national average of 6.9 and 2.7 respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-CrimeFigs_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrimeFigs-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> The number of sexual offences was 0.9, in line with the national average.<sup id="cite_ref-CrimeFigs_106-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrimeFigs-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> The national average of violence against another person was 16.2 compared to the York average of 17.5.<sup id="cite_ref-CrimeFigs_106-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrimeFigs-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> The figures for crime statistics were all recorded during the 2006–07 financial year.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="wikitable floatright" style="margin-left: 1em; width: 30em; font-size: 90%;">

<th><a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_and_the_Humber" title="Yorkshire and the Humber">Yorkshire<br />and the<br />Humber</a><sup id="cite_ref-auto_101-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup></th>

<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Inside_York_Minster.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Inside_York_Minster.jpg/170px-Inside_York_Minster.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="256" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Inside_York_Minster.jpg/255px-Inside_York_Minster.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Inside_York_Minster.jpg/340px-Inside_York_Minster.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="3008" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Inside_York_Minster.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Nave of <a href="/wiki/York_Minster" title="York Minster">York Minster</a>.</div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_York" title="Religion in York">Religion in York</a></div>
<p>Christianity is the religion with the largest following in York, with 59.5% residents reporting themselves as Christian in the 2011 census. The percentages following each non-Christian religion were all below the national average for England, but those responding as "No Religion" were higher than the national average.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Archbishop_of_York_John_Sentamu.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Archbishop_of_York_John_Sentamu.jpg/220px-Archbishop_of_York_John_Sentamu.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="336" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b1/Archbishop_of_York_John_Sentamu.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="262" data-file-height="400" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Archbishop_of_York_John_Sentamu.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Archbishop of York <a href="/wiki/John_Sentamu" title="John Sentamu">John Sentamu</a></div></div></div>
<p>There are 33 active <a href="/wiki/Anglican" class="mw-redirect" title="Anglican">Anglican</a> churches in York, which is home to the <a href="/wiki/Archbishop_of_York" title="Archbishop of York">Archbishop of York</a> and <a href="/wiki/York_Minster" title="York Minster">York Minster</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Mother_Church" class="mw-redirect" title="Mother Church">Mother Church</a> and administrative centre of the <a href="/wiki/Province_of_York" title="Province of York">northern province</a> of the Church of England and the <a href="/wiki/Diocese_of_York" title="Diocese of York">Diocese of York</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
York is in the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" class="mw-redirect" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholic</a> <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Middlesbrough" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Middlesbrough">Diocese of Middlesbrough</a>, has eight Roman Catholic churches and a number of different Catholic religious orders.<sup id="cite_ref-Middiocese_109-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Middiocese-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Leaders of different Christian denominations work together across the city, forming a network of churches known as One Voice York.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Other Christian denominations that are active in York include the <a href="/wiki/Religious_Society_of_Friends" class="mw-redirect" title="Religious Society of Friends">Religious Society of Friends</a> who have three <a href="/wiki/Friends_meeting_house" title="Friends meeting house">meeting houses</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Methodist" class="mw-redirect" title="Methodist">Methodists</a> within the York Circuit of The Methodist Church York and Hull District,<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Unitarianism" title="Unitarianism">Unitarians</a>. St Columba's <a href="/wiki/United_Reformed_Church" title="United Reformed Church">United Reformed Church</a> in Priory Street, originally built for the <a href="/wiki/Presbyterians" class="mw-redirect" title="Presbyterians">Presbyterians</a>, dates from 1879.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> York’s only Mosque is located in the <a href="/wiki/Layerthorpe" title="Layerthorpe">Layerthorpe</a> area, and the city also has a <a href="/wiki/UK_Islamic_Mission" title="UK Islamic Mission">UK Islamic Mission</a> centre.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> Various <a href="/wiki/Buddhism" title="Buddhism">Buddhist</a> traditions are represented in the city and around York.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=York&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Yorkshire_Museum,_York,_England-23March2005.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Yorkshire_Museum%2C_York%2C_England-23March2005.jpg/220px-Yorkshire_Museum%2C_York%2C_England-23March2005.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Yorkshire_Museum%2C_York%2C_England-23March2005.jpg/330px-Yorkshire_Museum%2C_York%2C_England-23March2005.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Yorkshire_Museum%2C_York%2C_England-23March2005.jpg/440px-Yorkshire_Museum%2C_York%2C_England-23March2005.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1536" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Yorkshire_Museum,_York,_England-23March2005.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_Museum" title="Yorkshire Museum">Yorkshire Museum</a> is based in the city – tourism is an important contributor to York's economy</div></div></div>
<p>York's economy is based on the <a href="/wiki/Service_industry" class="mw-redirect" title="Service industry">service industry</a>, which in 2000 was responsible for 88.7% of employment in the city.<sup id="cite_ref-NOMIS_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NOMIS-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> The service industries include public sector employment, health, education, finance, information technology (IT) and tourism that accounts for 10.7% of employment. Tourism has become an important element of the economy, with the city offering a wealth of historic attractions, of which <a href="/wiki/York_Minster" title="York Minster">York Minster</a> is the most prominent, and a variety of cultural activities. As a holiday destination York was the 6th most visited English city by UK residents (2014–16)<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> and the 13th most visited by overseas visitors (2016).<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg/220px-Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg/330px-Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg/440px-Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2400" data-file-height="1600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Tour_boats_on_the_River_Ouse.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Tour boats offer visitors a glimpse of the city from another perspective</div></div></div>
<p>A 2014 report, based on 2012 data,<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> stated that the city receives 6.9 million visitors annually; they contribute £564 million to the economy and support over 19,000 jobs.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> In the 2017 Condé Nast Traveller survey of readers, York rated 12th among The 15 Best Cities in the UK for visitors.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg/220px-Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg/330px-Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg/440px-Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2400" data-file-height="1600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Morris_dancers_York_8667.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Morris dancers entertain tourists in King's Square near The Shambles</div></div></div>
<p>Unemployment in York was low at 4.2% in 2008 compared to the United Kingdom national average of 5.3%.<sup id="cite_ref-NOMIS_116-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NOMIS-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> The biggest employer in York is the City of York Council, with over 7,500 employees. Employers with more than 2,000 staff include <a href="/wiki/Aviva" title="Aviva">Aviva</a> (formerly Norwich Union Life), <a href="/wiki/Network_Rail" title="Network Rail">Network Rail</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northern_(train_operating_company)" title="Northern (train operating company)">Northern</a>, York Hospitals NHS Trust and the <a href="/wiki/University_of_York" title="University of York">University of York</a>. Other major employers include <a href="/wiki/British_Telecom" class="mw-redirect" title="British Telecom">British Telecom</a>, <a href="/wiki/CPP_Group" title="CPP Group">CPP Group</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nestl%C3%A9" title="Nestlé">Nestlé</a>, <a href="/wiki/NFU_Mutual" title="NFU Mutual">NFU Mutual</a> and a number of railway companies.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Former_Savings_Bank,_St_Helen%27s_Square,_York.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Former_Savings_Bank%2C_St_Helen%27s_Square%2C_York.jpg/220px-Former_Savings_Bank%2C_St_Helen%27s_Square%2C_York.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="148" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Former_Savings_Bank%2C_St_Helen%27s_Square%2C_York.jpg/330px-Former_Savings_Bank%2C_St_Helen%27s_Square%2C_York.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Former_Savings_Bank%2C_St_Helen%27s_Square%2C_York.jpg/440px-Former_Savings_Bank%2C_St_Helen%27s_Square%2C_York.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1895" data-file-height="1272" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Former_Savings_Bank,_St_Helen%27s_Square,_York.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Commerce accounts for a large part of the city's economy.</div></div></div>
<p>Today's economic position is very different from the 1950s, when its prosperity was based on chocolate manufacturing and the railways. This position continued until the early 1980s when 30% of the workforce were employed by just five employers and 75% of manufacturing jobs were in four companies.<sup id="cite_ref-FYGREPORT_124-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FYGREPORT-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> Most industry around the railway has gone, including the carriage works (known as <a href="/wiki/ABB_Group" title="ABB Group">Asea Brown Boveri</a> or ABB at the time of closure), which at its height in the 1880s employed 5,500 people, but closed in the mid-1990s.<sup id="cite_ref-FYGREPORT_124-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FYGREPORT-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> York is the headquarters of the confectionery manufacturer Nestlé York (formerly Nestlé Rowntrees) and home to the <i><a href="/wiki/KitKat" class="mw-redirect" title="KitKat">KitKat</a></i> and eponymous <a href="/wiki/Yorkie_(chocolate_bar)" title="Yorkie (chocolate bar)"><i>Yorkie</i> bar</a> chocolate brands. <a href="/wiki/Terry%27s" title="Terry&#39;s">Terry's</a> chocolate factory, makers of the <i><a href="/wiki/Terry%27s_Chocolate_Orange" title="Terry&#39;s Chocolate Orange">Chocolate Orange</a></i>, was located in the city; but it closed on 30 September 2005, when production was moved by its owners, <a href="/wiki/Kraft_Foods" title="Kraft Foods">Kraft Foods</a>, to Poland. The historic factory building is situated next to the Knavesmire racecourse.
</p><p>On 20 September 2006, Nestlé announced that it would cut 645 jobs at the Rowntree's chocolate factory in York.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcrown_126-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcrown-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> This came after a number of other job losses in the city at <a href="/wiki/Aviva" title="Aviva">Aviva</a>, <a href="/wiki/British_Sugar" title="British Sugar">British Sugar</a> and Terry's chocolate factory.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcjobs_127-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcjobs-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, the employment situation in York remained fairly buoyant until the effects of the <a href="/wiki/Late_2000s_recession" class="mw-redirect" title="Late 2000s recession">late 2000s recession</a> began to be felt.<sup id="cite_ref-pressjobs_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pressjobs-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Aviva,_York.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Aviva%2C_York.jpg/220px-Aviva%2C_York.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Aviva%2C_York.jpg/330px-Aviva%2C_York.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Aviva%2C_York.jpg/440px-Aviva%2C_York.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1394" data-file-height="930" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Aviva,_York.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Aviva" title="Aviva">Aviva</a> Building – York is home to the office of one major company.</div></div></div>
<p>Since the closure of the carriage works, the site has been developed into offices. York's economy has been developing in the areas of science, technology and the <a href="/wiki/Creative_industries" title="Creative industries">creative industries</a>. The city became a founding National Science City with the creation of a <a href="/wiki/Science_park" title="Science park">science park</a> near the <a href="/wiki/University_of_York" title="University of York">University of York</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> Between 1998 and 2008 York gained 80 new technology companies and 2,800 new jobs in the sector.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Regional <a href="/wiki/Gross_value_added" title="Gross value added">gross value added</a> figures for York, at 2005 basic prices in millions of <a href="/wiki/Pounds_sterling" class="mw-redirect" title="Pounds sterling">pounds sterling</a>, are:<sup id="cite_ref-strgv_131-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-strgv-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
